London Naval Conference and League of Nations Relationship 47

Since the Treaty of Versailles was concluded and the League of Nations established, the first chapter of the Treaty of Versailles, which is the entire covenant of the League of Nations, shows that the representatives of the negotiating countries at that time spared no effort to find ways to eliminate the scourge of war and maintain peace. Unfortunately, the articles of the covenant were brief, and interpretations were often divergent. Although governments could request interpretations from the International Court of Justice in The Hague at any time, the power of restraint was difficult to impose on the world, and criticism often blamed the League for maintaining peace in name only, failing to devise practical measures. This was not without reason. Last September, at the General Assembly of the League of Nations, British Foreign Secretary Arthur Henderson and Chinese Dr. Wu Chao-chu each proposed amendments and interpretations to the articles of the covenant, leading to the establishment of a special committee to amend the covenant. This was also due to the recognition of the issue.

The London Naval Conference was primarily aimed at discussing the reduction and limitation of naval forces of the five major participating powers, but whether the naval forces of each country could be reduced and limited depended entirely on whether each country's own security concerns were resolved. Since the European War, there have been numerous international disarmament conferences, but the results have often been unsatisfactory. The point of contention lies here. For example, France's financial resources are far inferior to those of Britain and the United States, so it not only maintains vigilance against the naval power of Britain and the United States, but also harbors constant fear of its eastern neighbor Italy and a resurgent Germany. To maintain its existing position along its coast and in the Mediterranean, France has had to abandon the policy of large battleships and focus on building submarines as a means of defense. Therefore, at each disarmament conference, France insists on resolving the issue of security guarantees first. Given France's position and interests, its reasons are indeed not entirely unreasonable. At this London Naval Conference, the French representatives again strongly advocated for an interpretation of Article 16 of the Covenant of the League of Nations. According to a Reuters dispatch from London the other day, British Prime Minister MacDonald and French Foreign Minister Briand met to discuss the political issues of the Naval Conference, and as a result, an agreement has been reached on the interpretation of Article 16 of the Covenant of the League of Nations, which is related to French security. Since France has been fighting for security issues for years, and the League of Nations Covenant has been criticized for the security issues of member states, now that the Naval Conference has been able to satisfy France's wishes, France may agree with the participating powers on the policy of naval reduction. By extension, the Special Committee for the Amendment of the Covenant of the League of Nations can also use this as a basis for further discussion to achieve a satisfactory amendment of the Covenant. The result is not only related to the London Naval Conference. The original text of Article 16 of the Covenant of the League of Nations is recorded on the left for the reader's reference.

"Should any Member of the League resort to war in disregard of its covenants under Articles 12, 13 or 15, it shall ipso facto be deemed to have committed an act of war against all other Members of the League, which hereby undertake immediately to subject it to the severance of all trade or financial relations, the prohibition of all intercourse between their nationals and the nationals of the covenant-breaking State, and the prevention of all financial, commercial or personal intercourse between the nationals of the covenant-breaking State and the nationals of any other State, whether a Member of the League or not.

It shall be the duty of the Council in such case to recommend to the several governments concerned what effective military, naval or air force the Members of the League shall severally contribute to the armed forces to be used to protect the covenants of the League.

The Members of the League agree, further, that they will mutually support one another in the financial and economic measures which are taken under this Article, in order to minimize any loss or inconvenience resulting therefrom, and that they will mutually support one another in resisting any special measures aimed at one of their number by the covenant-breaking State, and that they will take the necessary steps to afford passage through their territory to the forces of any of the Members of the League which are co-operating to protect the covenants of the League.

Any Member of the League which has violated any covenant of the League may be declared to be no longer a Member of the League by a vote of the Council concurred in by the Representatives of all the other Members of the League represented thereon."

Page 9

Eighty-Fifth Meeting of the Legislative Yuan 48

The Legislative Yuan held its eighty-fifth meeting today (19th) at 8:00 AM. The following members were present: Jiao Yitang, Chen Zhaoying, Lin Bin, Chiang Song Meiling, Tao Xuan, Miao Bin, Shao Yuanchong, Sun Jingya, Lou Tongsun, Wu Shangying, Zhang Zhihan, Wang Yongbin, Lü Zhiyi, Liu Guantun, Zhuang Songfu, Lu Zhonglin, Liu Jixue, Luo Ding, Deng Zhaoyin, Wei Tingsheng, Zhang Fengjiu, Fu Bingchang, Chen Changheng, Liu Kejun, Fang Juehui, Zhu Hezhong, Liu Jingxin, Zheng Kaichen, and Wei Huai, totaling twenty-nine people. Hu Hanmin presided over the meeting. The following items were discussed: (1) The Art Protection Ordinance was resolved to be submitted to the Legal System Committee for review. (2) The Foreign Affairs Committee of the Yuan reported on the review of the Sino-Czech Friendship and Commercial Treaty, which was resolved to be passed according to the review report. (3) The Legal System Committee of the Yuan reported on the review of the amendment to Article 7 of the Communist Self-Surrender Law, which was resolved to be amended and passed according to the review report. The text of Article 7 was changed to "Self-surrender should be made to the court or other official agency after being approved by the local senior party department."

Fu Bingchang Lectures on Important Issues in the Relatives and Inheritance Sections of the Civil Code 49

The Civil Code Drafting Committee of the Legislative Yuan is currently working on drafting the Relatives and Inheritance sections. However, these two sections are of utmost importance, and the points that should be resolved first have been submitted to the Central Political Council for resolution by Yuan President Hu Hanmin and Lin Sen. Hu also requested Committee Chairman Fu Bingchang to give a lecture during the Yuan's memorial week on the 14th to promote the attention of all members of the Yuan. The text of Fu's speech is excerpted below:

(Previous text omitted) What I intend to report on today is the situation in preparing to draft the Relatives and Inheritance sections, which is even more difficult to report on. Because the biggest issues in Relatives and Inheritance are issues such as family, husband and wife, and father and son, which are extremely important and relevant to the survival of society and the lives of the people. Moreover, people have different views on these issues, and there is no way to unify opinions. Here, I would like to make a few statements. First, the opinions reported today are not the result of discussions by the Civil Code Drafting Committee. Second, the Civil Code Drafting Committee has no absolute preconceived notions about these two sections. Frankly speaking, we feel that drafting the Relatives and Inheritance sections is even more difficult than the previous three sections. When drafting the previous three sections, it was just a matter of legislative technique. In principle, all countries are almost the same. Although the Property Rights section has some differences due to the circumstances of each country, it is still relatively easy. As for the Relatives and Inheritance sections, there are very few countries that are completely the same, because the Relatives and Inheritance Law of each country is based on the social, historical, and economic conditions of that country, and cannot be imitated by another country. The conditions in China are now changing all the time. Which condition should we use as the standard? This is a very difficult question. Because the principles of the Relatives Law and the Inheritance Law are mostly based on social and moral concepts, and social and moral concepts change with the times and with different environments, it is very difficult to set a standard. Today, I will only briefly raise a few issues for discussion. Within each issue, there are almost all irresolvable areas. First, is the issue of family. China has always adopted the clan system for the issue of family members. Will we maintain this system in the future, or will we overthrow this system? This is very difficult to decide. On this point, the benevolent see benevolence, and the wise see wisdom, and there is no unanimous opinion. On the side that advocates overthrow, this system is feudalistic, violates the party's principle of equality between men and women, and can foster habits of personal dependence. On the side that advocates maintaining, this system is a great advantage of our Chinese nation. The Chinese have always been a disorganized force, and they rely on this system to maintain cohesion. We must promote the concept of family in order to achieve the concept of nation. Chinese emigrants working abroad often want to return to their homeland, which is not without reason due to the concept of family. Moreover, in fact, whether the abolition of the clan system can be achieved temporarily is still a question. Some people also ask whether, after the clan system is abolished, will the woman take the man's surname, or will the man take the woman's surname, or will another surname be found? It is also very complicated. From this perspective, it seems that both those who advocate preservation and those who advocate abolition have their reasons. This is the first difficulty in drafting these two sections. Second, is the issue of marriage. Originally, from a scientific perspective, there are three problems in the world that cannot be solved: one is birth, the second is death, and the third is marriage. Just talking about the issue of marriage, it is said that marriage is based on love. How does love arise between men and women? This is a problem that scientists have no way to solve. Now we are asked to solve this marriage problem, isn't it a very difficult thing? In the past, lawmakers were very arbitrary in legislating on this issue, but in recent decades, lawmakers have gradually adopted scientific methods and abandoned arbitrary methods. Therefore, we must study from both the social situation and from a scientific perspective in order to determine the most appropriate method. However, studying this issue from a social perspective is already very difficult, and studying it from a scientific perspective is even more difficult. What are the difficulties from a social perspective? Because most people in the world have a great weakness. Anything that I don't like, I insist on saying that it doesn't exist. For many immoral things, it seems that they are unwilling to admit that they will happen or exist. But in fact, whether we like it or not, it still happens and still exists. Now that we want to study the issue of marriage, we shouldn't deceive ourselves. First, we must ask what the fundamental concept of marriage is. According to my observation, there are probably three types of concepts of marriage in the world: (1) believing that marriage is solely for sexual desire; (2) believing that marriage is for public life; (3) believing that marriage is for procreation. The legislation of all countries in the world cannot be separated from these three types. The first type of marriage is most prevalent in the United States in Europe and America. This is because it is influenced by religion. Saint Paul said that marriage can prevent fornication, which is what it means. Since marriage is for the purpose of lust, if this condition is violated, it is naturally the only reason for divorce. Therefore, there are many cases of divorce in the United States after marriage due to estrangement. According to the detailed statistics I have obtained, in 1923 alone, there were more than 1.2 million marriages and more than 160,000 divorces. On average, roughly 13 out of 100 people who get married divorce. In recent years, roughly 30 out of 100 people who get married divorce. With so many divorces, what is the result? Before 1923, there were 80,000 children under the age of ten who were homeless every year in the United States as a result. Now there should be more than 100,000. According to their criminal investigations, 80 out of 100 juvenile offenders are these homeless children. Now the United States government feels that this issue is very important and is trying to find a solution, but there is no appropriate method. This is the result of the first concept of marriage, which is solely for lust. The second type of marriage is to separate lust and marriage. This system is most common in France. Its fundamental concept is different from that of the United States, so there are relatively fewer cases of divorce. However, because lust and marriage are separated too much, there are also bad phenomena, such as the major problem of population decline. This is the result of the second concept, which is to take family as a condition for marriage. The third type, which takes procreation as the purpose of marriage, is the Chinese. There are fewer cases of divorce compared to other countries, but the principle of equality between men and women cannot be maintained, and women are mostly not free. Which of these three concepts should we adopt? Isn't this the most difficult problem? Now, although the United States insists on maintaining its first concept, and France insists on maintaining its second concept, they are both trying to avoid the bad results. There are considerable reasons for taking these two concepts as the goal, and there are also considerable shortcomings at the same time. Which method should we adopt? It is really difficult to decide. (To be continued)

Development of the Longhai Railway 50

▲ Extension of Branch Line on the Eastern Section

▲ Addition of a Freight Depot at Xuzhou Station

Qian Zongze, Director of the Longhai Railway Administration, recently formulated two plans to develop railway services. One plan involves constructing a branch line northward from Bayiji Station on the eastern section to Zaozhuang. The other plan involves building a freight depot at the East Xuzhou Station and constructing a connecting track. Surveys and cost estimates for both projects are complete. Qian departed from Xuzhou for Beijing today (the 17th) to seek approval from the Ministry of Railways for these plans. Bi La, the chief engineer of the railway, has also arrived in Xuzhou to assist Qian in carrying out these projects. However, problems persist with tenants leasing land from the Longhai Railway. The following is a record of the planned projects:

▲ Construction of Branch Line: Bayiji Station is a major station located south of Pi County on the eastern section of the railway, and northeast of Xuzhou. From this station, a branch line will be built northward, passing through Xin Pizhou to reach Taierzhuang on the bank of the Grand Canal, across from Zaozhuang. Zaozhuang is the location of the Zhongxing Coal Mine. The existing Lin-Zao branch line connects to Lincheng Station on the Jinpu Railway. However, the transportation of coal from this mine, which is usually done via the Jinpu Railway, is insufficient. The coal is of excellent quality and abundant. Qian plans to build a branch line from Bayiji to Lincheng, crossing the Grand Canal to connect with Zaozhuang. This line will transport coal via Dapu for export, balancing the transportation of Zhongxing coal and developing the commercial transportation of the Longhai Railway. Zhang Duchen, Chairman of the Zhongxing Coal Mining Company, who previously served as Superintendent of the Longhai Railway, strongly supports Qian's proposal. The two parties have had substantial discussions. The surveyed length of the entire line is approximately 31 kilometers, with an estimated construction cost of 1.1 million yuan. The route runs north-south between Bayiji and Zaozhuang.

▲ Construction of Freight Depot: The Xuzhou station of the Longhai Railway is located in the North Gate. Later, the East Gate became a key transportation hub, so land was purchased in the East Station for construction, but due to lack of funds, this construction has not happened. Now the station borrows from the Jinpu Railway depot and connecting track, and rents these out daily. These rentals cause conflicts at times. Qian plans to construct a freight depot on the originally purchased and leased land. The land is located west of the East Station, which has already developed into a marketplace. It is north of Dama Road and east of Zhongzheng Street, and west of Laibin Lane. This area contains approximately four to five hundred houses and shops. Piling is already underway, and orders to move are being given to the tenants, in order to solicit construction bids. Once this freight depot is completed, a connecting track will be built northward, directly connecting to the main line of the railway at Erbawa, which is about 500 meters in length. The completed track will facilitate the loading and unloading of goods. Platforms will be built on both the east and west sides, with an estimated total construction cost of approximately 30,000 yuan.

▲ Tenant Issues: There are currently no problems with the right of way for the branch line. The land for the freight depot was originally leased by the Longhai Railway authorities in the fourth year of the Republic (1915) to the Yuanda and Dacheng companies, who then subleased it to merchants and residents. The contract term was two years, specifying that the land should be vacated within two years, with relocation expenses provided by the railway, and that after two years, no compensation would be provided. However, due to their business interests, the tenants were greatly alarmed. On the 15th, 16th, and 17th, they held meetings at the East Station Public Welfare Charity Association, with approximately one thousand people attending. They resolved to petition the railway authorities to consider their business difficulties and exempt them from relocation in order to maintain their businesses. They also selected Yao Chengyi and ten others as representatives to petition the railway. If a resolution cannot be reached, they will petition the government. This dispute appears to require resolution. The text of the petition is appended below: "Representatives of the merchants of Zhongzheng Street, Yao Yi, Yu Donghai, Zhu Guiqi, Zhang Zhuchen, Sun Yunchang, Cao Ziting, Zhang Bitang, Hou Mutao, Lan Haiqiu, Bi Mengfu, etc., humbly petition for understanding and accommodation to preserve our businesses and alleviate our difficulties. We merchants have leased land next to Zhongzheng Street in this city to build houses and conduct business. The land originally belongs to the Longhai Railway and was leased by the Yuanda and Dacheng companies, who subleased it to us. We hoped that the market would thrive and we could share in the profits. Unexpectedly, yesterday we received a letter from the Yuanda and Dacheng companies, stating that the Longhai Railway has expansion plans and the Administration is urgently requesting the land, ordering us to completely demolish the houses north of Dama Road and east of Zhongzheng North Street and hand them over within a limited time. Upon hearing this news, we were struck with dismay, as if by a thunderbolt, and were unable to contain our fear. This is a matter of life and death for us and is not a loss to be compared lightly. If we speak only of the rules, we would not dare to disobey. But if we speak of the circumstances, we must respectfully present our hardships in detail to the Director. We merchants are not wealthy. It was not easy to build our houses at the beginning. The funds required were either obtained by selling our possessions or by borrowing at interest. Our entire families rely on this for their livelihood. Demolishing the houses would truly endanger our lives. We believe that the Director cares about the people's suffering and would not bear to focus on one aspect and allow us to be plunged into despair without finding a way to rescue us. Furthermore, the ring road around the city was originally built by the Director himself during his tenure as the head of the police department. All those who rely on this road for business sing his praises and say that the market of Zhongzheng Street was developed because of the Director. We believe that he would not bear to abandon his previous achievements and cause the people to feel resentful. We have heard that the Director is requisitioning the land for the purpose of adding a connecting track and building a freight depot. Fortunately, there is vacant land to the north that can be used to make arrangements. If you could find a way to preserve our houses, so that our businesses are not lost and the market is not damaged, we merchants would be eternally grateful, and the Director's merits would also be immortalized. Therefore, we jointly request that you grant us special consideration and accommodation, for which we will be eternally grateful." (17th)

Detailed Account of the Fierce Battle Between Troops and Bandits at Sian 51

Over two thousand bandits from Taihu occupied Sian town in Changxing County at 8 AM on the 15th. After joint suppression efforts by troops and police, Sian was recaptured at 8 AM on the 16th. All the bandits have scattered and fled. The fierce battle between troops and bandits and the aftermath are recorded separately below:

▲ Before the Robbery: Before the bandit disturbances, cases of kidnapping and robbery were frequently reported in the vicinity of Sian. The town's police force was very weak, and it was difficult to suppress the bandits because they were scattered. People had to let them roam freely in the countryside. A month ago, rumors were rampant in the town, claiming that over a thousand members of the "Guangde Big Sword Society" had arrived in the nearby mountains, causing panic and unrest. Later, someone named Wang, who had been a drill instructor for the Niudian Bridge Protection Corps, incited his followers, and many petty criminals joined him. The garrisoned troops and police were aware of this, so the town was under de facto martial law. After the firearms of the protection corps at Xiaoxikou, Xucang Bridge, and Xiayuan Ferry were seized by bandits, the situation in the town became extremely critical. People were startled several times a night, with sporadic gunfire continuing throughout the night. As a result, the wealthy moved elsewhere, and the streets were deserted soon after dusk.

▲ Commencement of Fierce Fighting: The headquarters of the Third Battalion of the Second Regiment of the Security Corps was stationed in Sian, with the Eighth and Ninth Companies defending the town and the Seventh Company stationed in Lincheng. On the 14th, the battalion headquarters received confidential reports that thousands of bandits had arrived in the Changqiao Pass area, with a tendency to attack Sian. In addition to ordering his men to be on strict alert, Battalion Commander Wang secretly ordered the Seventh Company, stationed in Lincheng, to return to Sian to strengthen the defense. The Seventh Company set off immediately upon receiving the order. Near the beach, they heard the sound of gunfire, which sounded as frequent as a string of pearls from a distance of several miles. The bandits had already opened fire with the Security Corps. Before the bandits attacked Sian, they had sent bandits disguised as hawkers and residents to infiltrate the market, first surrounding the entire Ninth Company of the Security Corps. The Eighth Company was operating in the market, fearing harm to the residents, so they withdrew from Sian, detouring to the beach to join the Seventh Company. Upon seeing this, the bandits launched a counterattack. Bullets flew like rain for a time, causing many deaths. After holding out for a long time, the Security Corps had no choice but to retreat to Tiangan Bridge. After a short rest, they retreated to Lincheng Bridge to regroup.

▲ Loss and Recapture: After the Seventh and Eighth Companies of the Security Corps retreated to Lincheng Bridge, the Ninth Company was isolated and difficult to defend. Although they fought bravely against the bandits, more than half of the soldiers had been killed or wounded, so they had to withdraw from Sian, and the entire town fell into the hands of the bandits. At this time, the 30th Regiment of the Fifth Division of the National Army stationed in Changxing heard the alarm and sent the First and Second Battalions, led by Battalion Commanders Feng and Lai, to march to Lincheng on foot. At about 6 PM, Hang Yi, commander of the anti-bandit forces in the Taihu area, arrived by boat and immediately ordered each unit to prepare food at 12 PM and depart at 2 AM. The National Army formed the left wing, the Security Corps formed the right wing, and the 11th Water Police Team, led by Squad Leaders He and Wang, supported the left and right wings, heading towards Sian. Near Kongshan, they encountered a large group of bandits, and fighting ensued. The National Army and the Security Corps then used machine guns and mortars to attack the bandits. The fierce battle lasted for four hours. The bandits suffered more than 300 deaths. Because the military and police fire was fierce and unstoppable, the bandit forces were unable to resist and scattered in retreat. The military and police recaptured Sian at 8 AM on the 15th.

▲ Investigation of Losses: The intensity of this suppression of bandits in Sian was unprecedented. Therefore, the losses of the military and police were also relatively heavy. The Security Corps suffered 30 to 40 casualties (the exact number is still unknown). The National Army and the Water Police suffered similar numbers. The bandits suffered 300 to 400 deaths. One false regimental commander and one deputy regimental commander were killed, and two false battalion commanders were captured alive. More than ten residents were killed or wounded. Major shops in Sian were looted by bandits, with losses exceeding 50,000 yuan. During the fierce battle, the Security Corps seized more than a hundred large swords from the bandits, stained with blood. It is unknown how many lives were poisoned by them.

▲ Aftermath Issues: After the recapture of Sian, Hang Yi, commander of the anti-bandit forces in the Taihu area, and Feng and Lai, battalion commanders of the 30th Regiment of the Fifth Division of the National Army, led their troops to station in the town. In addition to jointly issuing announcements and encouraging merchants and residents to resume business as usual, they also planned to convene residents to discuss the aftermath.

▲ Display of Bandit Leaders' Heads: After being repelled by the military and police, the bandits who occupied Sian scattered towards Meixi, Anji, Changqiao, Xianqiao, Dayun Temple, and other places, with each group numbering about one to two hundred people. Their combat strength was still strong, so the military and police around Lincheng Bridge were on high alert, and the market was extremely deserted. The false overall commander of the bandits, Zhang Minggao (formerly the head of the Changxing County Protection Corps), and the false division commander Chen Zhuangda, were still at large. The false marshals Fu and Wang had been beheaded and displayed to the public.

Zhejiang Security Corps Searches and Suppresses Bandits in Pinghu 52

Pinghu Correspondence: After the bandits led by Taibao Ashu robbed and looted the area bordering Pinghu County and Jiangsu Province, the provincial government dispatched a security corps to pursue and suppress them. The entire Second Battalion of the Seventh Regiment of the Security Corps, including the Fourth, Fifth, Sixth, and Special Companies, led by Battalion Commander Zhao, departed from Pinghu for Xincang. At 2 AM on the 16th, soldiers from the Ninth Company of the Third Battalion of the Third Regiment also arrived. At approximately 5 AM that morning, they divided into two routes from Xincang (one via Quanggong Pavilion, one via Xinmiao) to search and advance in a large encirclement. Battalion Commander Zhao led the Fourth Company and part of the Special Company, advancing from Xinmiao, Liujia Yankiao, Qingduian, Zhuanjiaowan, and returning to Yaqian. Company Commander Ding led the Fifth Company and part of the Special Company, going north from Quanggong Pavilion, passing through Zhujiadun, Zhujiaqiao, Zhangshaqiao to Yaqian. The Ninth Company of the Third Battalion of the Third Regiment then garrisoned Yaqian at 10 AM to guard the rear. The Xinmiao base

Page 10

had two patrol boats of the merchant-run anti-smuggling camp stationed there, which were the area of responsibility for Squad Leader Tao Xiaoda. Based on a confidential report, Battalion Commander Zhao suspected that this squad leader was colluding with bandits. After arriving in the town, he immediately sent someone with a note to summon him. He then found out that Tao was at home in Luwan Temple and secretly ordered several members of the wooden-hulled gun squad to take Tao into custody first. Then, he disarmed the two patrol boats. While on the ship, they found a "38" type Mauser rifle engraved with the words "Dongjiu Yamen Protection Corps," which had been robbed by bandits last year, and a police saber. When they reached the home of bandit leader Taibao Ashu, it was empty, and they burned the house to the ground. At Qingduian, they arrested fifteen suspected criminals in a teahouse and escorted them back with the team. While passing through Zhuanjiaowan, they searched the house of bandit leader Yan Shushen, finding nothing, and also burned down the house of this bandit in Zhuanjiaowan. Company Commander Ding's unit arrested six bandits, a bandit woman, and many stolen goods in the area north of Quanggong Pavilion and Zhujiadun, and escorted them back to Yaqian via Zhangshaqiao. When the two routes reached Yaqian, the Ninth Company of the Third Battalion had also arrived. After arriving in the town, Battalion Commander Zhao sent a team to arrest Zhu Chaoquan, a suspected collaborator of the bandits in the town, surrounding Zhu's house and searching it. Zhu was not at home, and only letters and photos were found. Zhu's father, Hui Shi, and Pei San were arrested and escorted along with the other criminals back to Xincang. Squad Leader Tao Xiaoda of the merchant-run anti-smuggling team was then taken to He by Battalion Commander Zhao, accompanied by a company of soldiers, for interrogation. Before Tao was sent to He, Tao's subordinates had telegraphed Lu Diankui, the head of the merchant-run anti-smuggling camp, who then telegraphed County Magistrate Fang to find a solution. Zhu Hushi and others had already been sent to the county for interrogation. Because the guards were tight-lipped, their confessions could not be found out. At around 9 AM on the 18th, over ten bandit ships, fully loaded with armed bandits, were discovered near Qingyang Hui in Xindai Town, Pinghu County, sailing from Pubei, seemingly heading towards Huzhu Nunnery, Shantang, and Liujia Yankiao. The Pinghu County government received the report and has strengthened its defenses.

Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture Requests Protection of Fishing Grounds 53

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mines stated that banditry is rampant in the offshore fishing grounds of this province. Last year, as the fishing season was approaching, it had submitted a request to the Provincial Government, which was forwarded to the Executive Yuan, ordering the Ministry of Military Affairs to order the naval fleet stationed in Shanghai to send small warships for protection. The fishing season is now approaching again, and piracy is even more severe than last year in the various fishing grounds. Recently, the "Haiying" fisheries protection warship was robbed at Shengshan, making more stringent protection necessary. Otherwise, the flames of piracy will intensify, and the livelihoods of fishermen will be cut off. It proposed to follow the precedent of last year and respectfully request that the Provincial Government forward a request to the Ministry of the Navy, ordering the fleet stationed in Shanghai to dispatch several small warships to various fishing areas to protect offshore fisheries in order to ensure safety. It is heard that it has submitted a report to the Provincial Government, requesting that it be forwarded.

Jiangsu Provincial Capital Construction Engineering Office 54

▲ Reorganized from the Provincial Capital Construction Committee

▲ One Director Appointed, Reporting Directly to the Construction Department

The Jiangsu Provincial Capital Construction Committee was previously reorganized into the Jiangsu Provincial Capital Construction Engineering Office, which is directly under the Construction Department. The organizational rules for the office were approved by the Provincial Government yesterday. The contents are as follows: (Article 1) The Provincial Capital Construction Engineering Office is directly subordinate to the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department. (Article 2) All design and engineering implementation related to the construction of the Jiangsu provincial capital shall be drafted by this office, and after approval by the Construction Department, it shall be executed by this office. (Article 3) The office shall have one director, who shall handle all affairs of the office under the command of the Director of the Construction Department. (Article 4) The office shall have three chief engineers, who shall handle the planning, review, and inspection of various projects under the command of the director. (Article 5) The office shall have an engineering section and a general affairs section, each with a section chief, who shall be concurrently held by a chief engineer, handling the affairs of each section under the command of the director. (Article 6) The engineering section shall have two sections for design and construction, with the following division of duties: (1) Design Section: Responsible for the planning and estimation of various construction projects in the provincial capital. (2) Construction Section: Responsible for the construction, repair, and maintenance of various construction projects in the provincial capital. (Article 7) Each section of the engineering section shall have a chief, concurrently held by a chief engineer or section chief, with several engineers, clerks, and workers. (Article 8) The general affairs section shall have several clerks and workers, who shall be responsible for documents, general affairs, accounting, and statistics, and shall also handle the investigation and suppression of public and private buildings in the provincial capital. (Article 9) The office may establish several surveyors, clerks, assistant surveyors, and supervisors as needed, depending on the nature of the work. (Article 10) If there are any matters not covered by these rules, they may be submitted to the Provincial Government Committee for discussion and amendment at any time. (Article 11) These rules shall be implemented upon approval and promulgation by the Provincial Government Committee.

Hebei Provincial Government Decides to Crack Down on Japanese Residents in Changli 55

▲ All Nine Japanese Households Sell Morphine

Ping Correspondence: Sun Huanlun, Director of the Hebei Provincial Department of Civil Affairs, reported to the Provincial Government Committee yesterday that: "Based on the instructions of the Provincial Government, the magistrate of Changli County reported that nine Japanese households reside in the county and specialize in selling morphine and other drugs, which cannot be banned. It is proposed to select spacious temples to accommodate those arrested for smoking opium and injecting morphine, but it would be necessary to provide each person with an allowance of eight cents per day. It is requested that approval be granted to disburse the expenses, after verification, from 70% of the fine revenue of the Escort Bureau. Please issue instructions to comply with these instructions, etc. Based on this, in addition to issuing instructions, it is hereby ordered that the department investigate, handle, and report back. This order, etc. In accordance with this, after reviewing the case, the county had previously submitted a separate report to the department, and instructions were issued to wait for the Provincial Government to review and handle. Based on the previous instructions and after further investigation, the original request from the county is divided into two points: (1) Japanese merchants have opened pharmacies in Changli and are privately selling drugs, making it impossible to investigate and prohibit them. Please propose measures to seriously negotiate, etc. How should these crackdown measures, which are related to foreign affairs, be regulated? It is necessary to propose them for compliance. (2) Strictly prohibit those who are caught using drugs, which is a thorough method. However, the request to disburse the allowance from 70% of the fine revenue of the Escort Bureau involves using judicial fines, which should be handled by the High Court in conjunction with the Finance Department. Are these appropriate? It is respectfully reported to you after recording the county's document. Please make a public decision." The decision was made: (1) All foreign-owned pharmacies that privately sell drugs should be strictly cracked down on. (2) The method is acceptable, but the allowance should be raised locally and is not allowed to use fines. The original report from the Changli County Magistrate is attached below: "The Deputy Director of the Public Security Bureau of this county, Liu Tianfa, reported that: After investigation, there are as many as nine Japanese households residing within the county's borders. Some have resided there for twenty or thirty years, and some have resided there for more than ten years. All of them are using the name of medical practice and selling medicine as a front, but in reality, they specialize in selling drugs such as morphine, cocaine, and heroin. According to investigations, although successive county magistrates and public security bureau directors have tried to ban them, they have often been forcibly taken back by the Shanhaiguan garrison troops after being arrested. Even if some were handed over to the Tianjin Foreign Affairs Office and then sent to the Japanese consulate for legal proceedings, the escorts often had not returned before the criminals had already returned to Changli and continued to sell drugs as before. According to recent investigations, not only people in the lower classes of our country are injecting morphine and using drugs, but also many in the middle and upper classes are addicted to this vice. The depth of its harm and the intensity of its damage will inevitably lead to the destruction of the nation and the extermination of the race. Since taking office, the Director has been deeply concerned and has been eager to strictly prohibit it in order to eliminate the scourge. However, due to diplomatic constraints, there is no good policy. Furthermore, the Japanese are extremely barbaric and unreasonable. Changli is not a treaty port, so how can these Japanese freely trade? Moreover, transporting and selling drugs is a violation of international law. After careful consideration, the Director believes that this kind of poison must not be allowed to spread arbitrarily. In addition to ordering the landlords of the Japanese who sell drugs to take back their houses within a limited time and not allow them to be rented, and strictly investigating and arresting the criminals who buy and use drugs and sending them to the county for punishment, could your government forward a protest to the Ministry of Civil Affairs of the Provincial Government and raise it with the Japanese consul? Changli has not been opened as a port, so Japanese merchants should be cracked down on in the territory. Furthermore, criminals arrested in the future should be transferred to the consulate for strict punishment in accordance with the law and should not be lightly released, which would violate international law, and the Japanese consulate should order the Japanese garrison in Shanhaiguan not to interfere arbitrarily. Are the proposed matters appropriate? It is respectfully requested that you review and forward them for the public convenience, etc. Based on this, after investigating the claim of the bureau director that as many as nine Japanese households reside within the county's borders and that they all use the name of selling medicine as a front but in reality specialize in selling morphine and various drugs, the situation is true. However, Changli is closer to Shanhaiguan, where there is a Japanese military police team stationed. Whenever the county government seizes Japanese who are selling drugs, the garrison troops come to Changli to demand their release. In previous years, there were even cases of forcibly demanding the return of criminals, and the county government was unable to handle them due to diplomatic relations. Although it sometimes reluctantly refused, once the criminal was sent to the Foreign Affairs Office and then transferred to the Japanese consulate, they were mostly sentenced to the lightest fine and then released. There was no serious punishment at all, and the travel expenses for sending the case were not cheap. Sometimes, the escorting officials had not even returned to the county before the criminals had already returned and resumed their business. If this continues, the impact on the opium ban will be no small matter. In order to eliminate the scourge and strictly enforce the ban, the county magistrate intends to request that the Provincial Government hold a meeting to discuss and decide on measures for serious negotiations in order to investigate and prohibit them. The county magistrate further requests that the county is close to Shanhaiguan, and Japanese merchants privately sell drugs at ordinary times, which is indeed very common. Moreover, Changyi is one of the five counties in Bay East, and the recovery of sovereignty was later than in other counties. Therefore, those who smoke opium and inject morphine are still frequently seen. However, eight or nine out of ten of the unemployed poor are involved. Those arrested are subject to fines, but the penalty cannot be applied due to not having the financial resources to pay. There is no special regulation providing a basis for imprisonment. If the arrestees do not receive their dosage of the drug, they develop severe diarrhea, resulting in unhygienic conditions, and overcrowding in prisons. Therefore, it is proposed that the arrestees should be gathered and detoxed in spacious temples with the medical care provided by the local missionary hospital. Each prisoner would require food worth eight cents a day. It is requested that the Provincial Committee meet to decide on whether it is appropriate to use 70 percent of the fines levied to pay for this. It is respectfully requested that your department review and instruct us to comply."

Three-Province Bandit Suppression Headquarters Moves from Fujian to Jiangxi 56

Nanchang Correspondence: Jin Handing, Commander-in-Chief of the Bandit Suppression in the three provinces of Jiangxi, Guangdong, and Fujian, arrived in the province from Beijing on the 10th and has been holding detailed discussions on bandit suppression plans with Chairman Lu and Brigade Commander Tang for several days. On the afternoon of the 11th, he and Chairman Lu also hosted a banquet for various military officers at the Provincial Government, during which the bandit suppression issue was discussed again. According to Jin's interview with reporters, the 12th Division will leave a unit in the Ninghua area of Fujian, and the majority of the Zhang and Tang Brigades have arrived in southern Jiangxi from Ruijin and Shicheng. The Yang Yingzhi and Xiao Xixian Regiments have been pursuing Zhu and Mao towards the Guangdong border. The Three-Province Bandit Suppression Headquarters also departed from Tingzhou, Fujian, on the 10th and arrived in Ganzhou. I (Jin referring to himself) will go to Ganzhou from the province in the shortest possible time to be responsible for clearing the scattered bandits in Ganzhou, Yudu, Xingguo, Ningdu, and other counties, and for flanking Zhu and Mao with the Guangdong army. Furthermore, bandits and communists are still active along the Gan River in Taihe and Wan'an, Ganzhou, and civilian and steamboat traffic has been disrupted for several months. Master Zhang has now ordered Peng's Regiment of the Zheng Brigade to move up the Gan River from Taihe, and one regiment of the 35th Brigade to move down the river from Ganzhou, flanking each other and clearing the scattered bandits obstructing transportation in order to alleviate the obstruction of the traveler's feet. After being severely suppressed by Zhu's Brigade and Yi's Regiment of the 18th Division and Deng Ying's Brigade in Anfu, Wanzai, Xinyu, Fenyi, Yichun, and other places, the Peng bandits in western Jiangxi are in a miserable state. The Provincial Government received a telegram from Brigade Commander Deng yesterday, reporting that the Peng bandits were unable to resist the pressure and that some had hidden in the Wugong Mountains, while others had fled to Yongxin via Lianhua. Orders have been telegraphed to Wang's and Li's Regiments in Fenyi and Yichun to pursue them. (April 11)

東明縣未便劃歸山東 57

▲ The Executive Yuan has instructed the Shandong Provincial Government to take note.

Jinan Correspondence: Although the Yellow River project in Dongming County, Hebei Province, south of the Yellow River, is being carried out in Hebei, once a breach occurs, it will inundate the area of Caozhou, Shandong. The Provincial Government recently submitted a request to the central government, based on the suggestion of Ge Xiangyi, a member of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, to place Dongming County under the jurisdiction of Shandong. Yesterday, the Provincial Government received an order from the Executive Yuan rejecting the request. The order stated: "Upon investigation, the Executive Yuan previously received a request from the Shandong Provincial Government, forwarded from Ge Xiangyi of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, suggesting that the river works on the south bank of the Yellow River in Hebei Province and Dongming County be placed under the jurisdiction of Shandong for review and instructions. The Executive Yuan then forwarded it to the Ministry of Interior for deliberation and reply. According to the reply, the original suggestion was made because the Liuzhuang area on the south bank of the Yellow River in Hebei Province is particularly dangerous, and other areas are also unsafe. No matter where the danger lies, the harm is all in Shandong. From the 6th to the 18th year of the Republic of China, there were five breaches, causing great losses to the people of western Shandong. The Hebei Provincial Government has been perfunctory in managing the dams and flood prevention, and has not paid attention. Therefore, it is proposed to place Dongming County and the areas of Changyuan and Puyang counties south of the Yellow River under the jurisdiction of Shandong Province, and to place the river works on the south bank of the province under the management of Shandong. Upon investigation, the section of the Yellow River within Hebei Province has frequently been in danger, which is indeed a fact. However, almost the entire Dongming County in Hebei Province is south of the Yellow River, and parts of Changyuan and Puyang counties are also on the south bank of the Yellow River. The proposal to place the south bank of the Yellow River in Hebei under the jurisdiction of Shandong Province, and to place Dongming and other places under the jurisdiction of the province, would divide the river works on both banks into two, each looking after its own interests, which may lead to more disputes. Furthermore, regarding the Yellow River affairs, the National Government has previously ordered the establishment of the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission, which has already established a preparatory office. According to Article 1 of the commission's organizational regulations, the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission is directly under the National Government and is in charge of the entire Yellow River and its tributaries, surveying, dredging, irrigation, and all water conservancy fundraising and construction matters. Regarding the Yellow River project, it can be planned and managed as a whole after the commission is formally established. All suggestions can be temporarily shelved. As for the current issues of repairing, managing, and preventing dangers, we request that your esteemed Executive Yuan instruct the two provincial governments to effectively negotiate and cooperate to maintain the current situation and avoid disputes. Please review and approve." It should be approved and handled as discussed.

黑省舉行悲壯追悼會 58

▲ A solemn memorial service was held in Heilongjiang Province.

▲ More than 10,000 people attended the ceremony.

▲ Fallen soldiers were enshrined in the Martyrs' Shrine.

Heilongjiang, 8th: The Provincial Government deeply regrets that many brave and loyal generals and officers were killed in the defense against Russia last year. Liaoning held a memorial service on the 5th, but Heilongjiang Province is far away, making it inconvenient to participate. In addition, many of the soldiers killed last year were elites of the Heilongjiang army, so Heilongjiang Province also held a memorial service to comfort the departed souls. The date was from April 5th to 7th. A preparatory office was set up in advance to organize the event. A very large mat shed was erected in front of the Martyrs' Shrine in Pangsha Park, and 10,000 admission tickets were printed and distributed to all sectors of society. At 9 a.m. on the 5th, representatives from various provinces, central government representatives, and representatives from various cities and counties in Heilongjiang Province arrived. Together with military police, merchants, and civilians, there were more than 10,000 people attending the ceremony. Wan Fulin, dressed in mourning clothes, personally presided over the memorial service. The memorial service included: (1) Participants, led by the chief celebrant, bowed three times to the portrait of the Premier, while the military police fired their guns. (2) The Premier's will was read aloud, followed by three minutes of silence. (3) A report on the purpose of the meeting was given. (4) Representatives of the Chairman of the Central Government, representatives of various ministries and departments, representatives of the Commander-in-Chief of the Northeast, and representatives of the civil and military organs of various provinces and regions offered sacrifices. (5) Various legal entities offered sacrifices. (6) The Deputy Commander and Chairman of the province led the members of the Provincial Government and various officials of the province to offer sacrifices. (7) Speakers delivered speeches. (8) Slogans were chanted, and photos were taken. The ceremony concluded. On this day, all participants expressed their sorrow. When the bereaved families of Brigade Commander Han Guangdi and Regiment Commanders Wei Changlin and Zhang Lin offered sacrifices, they cried uncontrollably. Everyone present, starting with Wan Fulin, shed many tears. From 9 a.m. on the 6th, representatives from various provinces, regions, cities, and towns, as well as military police, arrived and offered sacrifices in shifts. Students from various schools also came to offer sacrifices, totaling six to seven thousand people. At 11 a.m. on the 7th, Wan Fulin personally led the people from all parties who came to offer sacrifices to send the memorial tablets into the Martyrs' Shrine. The order was as follows: (1) Ushers guided the chief celebrant to the altar to take his place. (2) Cannons were fired. (3) Incense was offered. (4) Libations were poured. (5) Mournful music was played. (6) Hats were removed and bows were made. (7) Ushers distributed and carried the memorial tablets of the fallen soldiers into the shrine. (8) The chief celebrant led a company of military police, a company of cavalry, a company of infantry, the entire military band, and full ceremonial guards, lamas, monks, Taoists, scriptures, incense, flowers, and sacrificial offerings, arranged in escort. (9) They passed through Guanyuan Hospital Hutong, turned east and north to Xicheng Ditch, then turned from Xicheng Ditch to South Street, and from Post Office Hutong west to pass through Caishenmiao Street and enter the Martyrs' Shrine in the park. (10) (1) Enshrinement, with rituals performed as appropriate. After the ceremony, the deities were sent into the shrine. Along the way, they passed through the main streets, and the onlookers were like walls. Military police and students shouted slogans: (1) The spirit of the fallen soldiers is immortal. (2) The fallen soldiers sacrificed for the country and the people. (3) The fallen soldiers are models for Chinese soldiers. (4) Continue the spirit of the fallen soldiers to recover the rights to the China Eastern Railway. (5) Realize the Three Principles of the People. (6) Long live the Republic of China. The cries were extremely tragic, and those who heard them were all saddened and shed tears.

Local Communications

Songjiang 60

Measures to Expand the Police Force: The current police force in this county consists of only one company. With rampant bandits in the four villages, it is felt that the defense is inadequate. At the second county administrative meeting of this session, the county government specifically discussed measures to expand the police force. It is proposed to form a large company in accordance with the provincial-level B police force regulations. In addition to the existing company, two more companies will be recruited, including four squads of rifles and one squad each of machine guns and mortars, in order to increase strength. However, the estimated start-up cost is more than 50,000 yuan, and the recurring cost is more than 100,000 yuan. Local public funds are exhausted, and the land value surcharge has reached one percent. Regarding the funding method, it is proposed to solicit donations from wealthy households for the start-up cost in one lump sum, and to implement a household registration tax for the recurring cost. The collection method is to divide the 80,000 households in the county into four classes, excluding those who are poor and unable to pay: (1) Those with assets of 50,000 yuan or more are in the special class, paying 16 yuan per year, accounting for 200 households. (2) Those with assets of 10,000 yuan or more are in the first class, paying 8 yuan per year, accounting for 3,000 households. (3) Those with assets of 5,000 yuan or more are in the second class, paying 4 yuan per year, accounting for 10,000 households. (4) Those with assets of 1,000 yuan or more are in the third class, paying 2 yuan per year, accounting for 6,800 households. The collection will be carried out quarterly each year. As for the one-time collection of start-up fees, the special class will pay an average of 50 yuan per household, and the first class will pay an average of 20 yuan per household, which will collect approximately 70,000 yuan, which is sufficient for application. After review, the conference passed the resolution and will implement it once approved.

Farmers in Shanyang Were Robbed and Reported to the County: On the evening of the 11th, eight or nine bandits with painted faces and weapons suddenly came to the home of Zhou Ala, a farmer in Wujia, Shanyang Township, which belongs to the county. They broke down the door and entered, first tying up the couple and searching the inner room. All the cash, more than 30 yuan, and more than 50 pieces of clothing were robbed.

Maple Creek Thief Arrested and Sent to Songjiang: Wang Yusheng, director of the Maple Creek Public Security Bureau, captured Jiangbei serial thieves Yao Yuelu and Yao Daishi, etc., as well as a large number of stolen goods, including 119 pieces of clothing, silver ornaments, foreign currency, and cotton quilts. Special police officers were dispatched to escort the people and goods to the county government for interrogation and detention pending disposition.

Suzhou 61

Henan Gang Bandit Leader Arrested in Shanghai: The Taihu Bandit Suppression Headquarters reported that the Henan Gang bandit leader Tian Mingguang (nickname Tian Kuaizi), after being defeated by government troops, abandoned the gang and hid in No. 24 Dapufang, Jin Shenfu Road, French Concession, Shanghai. The headquarters requested that personnel be dispatched to arrest him immediately. Commander Hu sent Adjutant Li Yan, intelligence officer Shao Henglong, and water police squad leader Du Jingwu, etc., by car to Shanghai on the evening of the 18th. On the 19th, they notified the French Concession police and went to the address to arrest the bandit Tian Mingguang. He was immediately escorted to the Longhua Songhu Garrison Headquarters for interrogation and disposition. Adjutant Li and others returned to Suzhou in the afternoon to report.

Bandit Ships Arrive in Chefang Dayao: The county government received a report on the afternoon of the 19th that more than ten bandit ships with more than a hundred bandits had arrived in the Dayao area of Chefang Township, intending to harass the area. Magistrate Huang ordered the county police team to rush to pursue and arrest them.

County Finance Bureau Seeks Loans: Yuan Xiaogu, Director of the Wuxian County Finance Bureau, recently found that the miscellaneous taxes collected for the busy season have been transferred to the province or allocated for various uses. Currently, there is an urgent need for 30,000 yuan owed to the Education Department, 19,500 yuan allocated by the provincial government to subsidize the Suzhou municipal government, 16,000 yuan for the water public security team, and various expenses for the prison and county education, totaling 88,000 yuan. This money has not yet been secured, but it urgently needs to be allocated. He discussed this with Magistrate Huang and proposed that the two heads of the county bureau should write to the General Chamber of Commerce to borrow 88,000 yuan from the silver and money industries for a period of six months, with the principal and interest to be repaid from the silver collected during the busy season of the 19th year. However, the silver and money industries were quite reluctant to provide this loan because it had not been approved by the Finance Department.

Opening Up Guangmu Road Hinders Silkworm Farming: The Wuxian County Construction Bureau is opening up Guangmu Road (Guangfu to Mudu), which is currently underway. However, most of the villagers in the area plant mulberry trees, which is now the time to raise silkworms. It is inevitable that this will hinder the livelihood of farmers. Therefore, Zhang Hong, the head of the Guangfu District, submitted a petition to the county government on the 19th, proposing to first open up the paddy fields on the flat road, and to temporarily set a line standard for the mulberry fields, and then build it after the silkworm season is over. Magistrate Huang immediately instructed the Construction Bureau to review and reply.

Series of Robbery Cases in Xueshan Township: Xueshan Township, Qingpu County, borders Wuxian County. On the 18th, dozens of lake bandits arrived and robbed the homes of Jin Ben Da, Xu Jinrong, and others, and injured the victims. The county magistrate of Qingpu County, Shen Yong, has consulted with the Wuxian County water and land authorities to strictly arrest them. In addition, more than ten bandits arrived in Hengjingluo Township, Wuxian County, on the night of the 14th and robbed the homes of farmers Zhu Baoxing and others.

After approval by the Department, the county was ordered to dismiss him. After receiving the order, the county government dismissed Xu Yinshi, and Tao Changhua was appointed to act as his replacement.

German Inspection Group Arrives in Wuxi for Inspection: The German Industrial Inspection Group came to China for inspection, and after transiting from Shanghai to Nanjing, they will visit Zhenjiang. They were scheduled to arrive in Wuxi from Zhenjiang by train at 9:15 p.m. yesterday (19th). The County Chamber of Commerce and industry representatives such as Rong Desheng have prepared to receive them and will go to the station to welcome them. They will rest at the Washington Hotel. Police Team Arrests Communist Suspect: The county police team arrested Zhang Erbao, a suspected Communist, in Qingchengshi, No. 82, Northern Township the day before yesterday. He was escorted to the county government for interrogation yesterday.

Appeal to Ban Superstitious Businesses: The Paper Foil Industry Association of this county received a directive from the Department of Industry and Commerce through the County Chamber of Commerce, along with a copy of the measures to ban superstitious businesses. They were instructed to follow the ban and switch to other industries within one year. Therefore, yesterday afternoon, the association invited its members to hold a meeting at the Jiangjianshang Hall to discuss the measures. It was decided that this ban would hit their industry the hardest, and it was fundamentally related to the origin of the products in Zhejiang and Shaoxing. Moreover, Jiangsu Province is within the scope of sales. If the source is cut off, it will naturally be banned. However, hundreds of millions of workers in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and other provinces rely on this for a living. If it is banned, the people will have no means of survival. A public letter was sent to the County Chamber of Commerce to request the superiors to withdraw the national decree in order to maintain the livelihood of the people.

Resolutions of the District Chief Conference: Sun, the magistrate of this county, convened the fourth district chief conference at the Wenxi Hall of the County Government at 2 p.m. the day before yesterday to discuss all ongoing matters. The resolutions included: (1) The county's prisons urgently need to be expanded. Previously, an order was issued to raise 4,000 yuan. It was decided how to allocate the funds to each district. It was decided that each district should raise at least 150 yuan and submit it all by the end of this month. (2) The method of rent reduction for tenant farmers during the cocoon market this year was discussed. The tu zheng of each district should be elected by the people immediately. It was decided to proceed accordingly.

The First Battalion Passes Through Wuxi to Liyang to Suppress Bandits: Sian Town in Changxing County, Zhejiang Province, was captured by bandits on the 15th of this month. It has been recovered by the bandit suppression commander of the West District, Zhong Huan, who led his team to encircle and suppress the bandits. Fearing that the remaining bandits would disturb other counties, the headquarters telegraphed Liu Guanlong, battalion commander of the First Battalion of the 265th Regiment of the 133rd Brigade of the 45th Division, originally stationed in Yangzhou, to lead the entire battalion of officers and soldiers to Liyang to defend and suppress the bandits. The Wuxi County Government received a telegram from the Department of Civil Affairs yesterday, instructing it to quickly prepare boats. At 8:30 p.m., more than 500 soldiers of the First Battalion, led by Battalion Commander Liu, arrived in Xishi by six trains from the town, and immediately disembarked and headed to Liyang.

Difficulties in Wuxi-Changzhou Road Construction: The Wuxi-Changzhou Provincial Road, which was requisitioning labor for road construction, was originally scheduled to begin on the 15th of this month. Due to rain, it was postponed to the 18th. However, when staking, spraying, and printing gray lines, the people of Shouzhitown, Dongting Township, and Chajiaqiao, etc., in the tenth district, objected that the Construction Bureau changed the old road's previous straight path and instead sought a circular new route, believing that it was abandoning the near for the far. The villagers' representatives Zhu Mogu and Lu Zhongxian, etc., submitted petitions to the Department of Construction and the Construction Bureau, stating that the new route was entirely between the fields, which would require much land and bridge filling, making the project very large and far from the old route, which was detrimental to the public and harmful to the people. They requested that personnel be dispatched again to inspect the route in order to change the route. On the first day of requisitioning labor to start construction, the people of the 1278910th and other districts, which are near the route, were all holding a wait-and-see attitude. There are still many difficulties in starting construction. Yao Dixi, Director of the Construction Bureau, had a serious discussion with Magistrate Sun, but there was no adequate solution. It has now been decided to submit a report to the Provincial Department for review and decision.

Zhenjiang 66

Yangzhou 67

Beating Grandfather and Kidnapping Grandson Case: On the 10th of this month, Xue Shunxing's firewood shed at Mabaidu Wharf outside the South Gate was robbed, and the grandfather was killed and the grandson was kidnapped. It has now been heard that after the robbery, the victim did not dare to report to the authorities because the grandfather had already died and the grandson had not escaped danger. The authorities, in their duty, thoroughly investigated the matter. The bandit then threw the kidnapped boy, Jin Lingzi, into the pond near the firewood shed. The corpse floated on the surface of the water, which was very tragic. It is also heard that the Xue family has only this one grandfather and one grandson.

Implementing Examinations for Police Chiefs: Since the reorganization of the Jiangdu Public Security Bureau, each of the four branch offices in the city and suburbs has seven police chiefs. Now, according to the reorganized system, only six people are stipulated. One person must be laid off in each office. Director Zhao plans to convene the police chiefs of each branch office tomorrow (19th), and separately select several police officers and recruit police officers sent by the provincial training class, and take academic examinations together to select the best candidates.

Danyang 68

Reasons for the Arrest of Tang Wencui: Regarding the arrest of Tang Wencui, a teacher at the County Teachers' Experimental Primary School, it is now known that the teacher graduated from Nanjing Xiaozhuang Normal School and has only been working at the school for a few days. Because he had a letter to a certain lady in Wuxi, which contained many political meanings and involved the sealing of Xiaozhuang Normal School and damage to transportation, it was detected and arrested by a postal and telecommunications inspector. Magistrate Wu and Wang, the reviewing judge, secretly interrogated him once, and temporarily issued a detention order and telegraphed the province for instructions.

Gaoyou 69

Opening of the Trial of the Pawnshop Embezzlement Case: Ma Junqing, a local gentry, and He Shaonan, a well-known figure in the business community, jointly opened the North-South Lianghuang pawnshop in the Chengnian period. In the autumn of the 16th year, it was robbed by rebellious soldiers and suffered heavy losses, which led to its closure. Now Ma has found that He had embezzled funds, and filed a lawsuit with the county government. Yesterday (16th) at 7 p.m., the reviewing judge, Hu, opened the court for interrogation. Ma was unable to attend due to illness, so only the witnesses Zhu Xi and Zhang Zhongfu were interrogated along with He. At the end of the interrogation, it was ruled that He was indeed suspected of embezzlement, and it was ordered that he be detained first, pending investigation of the books and further verification. After a request, it was ordered to change to a security deposit of 1,000 yuan and a reliable business guarantor.

All Teachers and Staff Demand Salary: The educational funding in this county is extremely stretched. The salaries for February and March of this year have not yet been paid. All the teachers and staff in this city, because Director Chen was transferred to Yangzhou, went to the Education Bureau together at 4 p.m. yesterday to demand the payment of salaries owed during his term of office. Representatives Gao Fusun and others were temporarily elected to meet Director Chen in person for a long time. It was agreed that half a month's salary would be paid on the 25th of this month, and the rest would be worked hard to raise funds. The teachers and staff left the bureau one after another until 8 p.m.

Rugao 70

The bandit situation in the southern countryside has reignited. The county government, due to the urgency of city defense, had previously transferred the 8th detachment of the 3rd squadron stationed in the Motou area of the southern countryside, Liujia Ferry, to the city for joint defense. However, after the detachment was transferred to the city, the defense in that area suddenly became tense. The communist bandits held secret meetings, intending to riot. The brigade headquarters, upon receiving the report, immediately ordered the detachment to return to its original defense and also ordered the 1st and 2nd squadrons to assist in the suppression. Furthermore, the Shizhuang district office, due to the resurgence of bandit atmosphere, specially sent a district guard to the county to report a few days ago. Unexpectedly, he was killed by bandits in the Shuangfengyuan area.

Rice prices exceed twenty yuan. The rice price in this county is unusually high, gradually soaring. Currently, West Saigon rice has risen to twenty-one yuan and three jiao per dan, superior indica rice to twenty-one yuan and one jiao per dan, medium indica rice to twenty yuan and six jiao, and inferior indica rice to twenty yuan. Compared to the rice price last month, each dan has risen by one yuan and two jiao.

Eight robbery cases occurred in one night. In the Shaojiazhuang of the northwest township of the first district (urban area) of Rugao County, the home of carpenter Shi Ermu was broken into by more than twenty bandits on the night of the 14th. All the silver, clothing, ornaments, and other items in the house were looted. At the same time, the homes of Zhang Pingchen, Wang in Jijiazhuang, Zhang Zishi, Zhang Tangshi, Zhang Jinxiang, Jin Hengshan, and Huang Laoer in Yelin Township were all robbed. Furthermore, Zhang Erxiangzi, the guard of Zhang Zishi's and Zhang Tangshi's homes, and Wang Laoer were kidnapped and a ransom of 20,000 yuan was demanded.

Jiashan 71

Bandits on the Baimao River kidnap a woman. Last night, two bandit boats suddenly arrived at the Baimao River, eight li outside the eastern shed of Xitang. More than twenty bandits invaded the Jin family, looting at will. Finding no valuable items, they kidnapped the female head of the household, demanding a large sum for ransom. The bandits intended to kidnap her uncle's family, but they had moved away early to avoid trouble, so they suffered no losses.

Two more bandit boats arrive at Fanbang New Town. Yesterday, a group of bandits, about thirty boats, came from Punan and arrived at Fanbang New Town. After landing, they went ashore one after another, causing great panic in the area. It is said that they are remnants of Xu Tianxiong's gang.

Matchmaker kidnapped. Zhu Liquan, a resident of this county, hired Gu Shaochuan and Lu Longshan as matchmakers to betroth a daughter of the Yu Hui Yao family as a wife. On the 17th, they went to present the betrothal gifts. Unexpectedly, near Yu Hui, they suddenly encountered a bandit boat, which kidnapped the two matchmakers and looted all the betrothal gifts. Their whereabouts are unknown.

Huzhou 72

Bandits kidnap and shoot the victim. Yu Yutian, a farmer from other province, lives half a li from Niudian Bridge. At about 1:00 AM this morning, several bandit boats suddenly docked in the outer harbor. More than twenty bandits, each armed with guns, swarmed to Yu's house and slammed on the door. Yutian, hearing the alarm, immediately braced the door. However, due to the strength of the bandits, the door was broken open, and Yutian was shot. The bullet entered from below his right rib and exited from his back. They also tied up Yutian's seventy-year-old mother, searched at will, and looted all the clothes, silver, and nine dan of rice. Before leaving, they fired their guns as a show of force and took the hostage away by boat. Afterwards, Yutian's younger brother took Yutian to the Gospel Hospital in this city for treatment. However, due to the severity of the injuries, his life may not be saved.

Hangzhou 73

The First National Exhibition closes. At 9:00 AM yesterday, the Hangzhou National Goods Promotion Committee held the closing ceremony of the First National Goods Mobile Exhibition at the YMCA. More than 800 representatives from the Zhejiang Provincial Government, Hangzhou Municipal Government, Family Industry Society, and other agencies, groups, and factories attended. Chairman Ruan Jihou reported, stating briefly that the association had been preparing since the 25th of last month and had encountered various difficulties with incomplete equipment. Now, after 14 days, the term has expired, so the closing ceremony is being held. He expressed gratitude for the assistance from all sectors and thanked the YMCA for lending the premises, especially for their enthusiasm. Representatives from various agencies, such as Qian Jingxi and Jiang Senyu, then delivered speeches and the ceremony concluded.

Shangyu 74

Shangyu News Moves to Shanghai. Zhu Yunwu, Jue Nong Hu Yuzhi and other fellow townsmen from Shangyu living in Shanghai, invited comrades to found the Shangyu Xunkan in Shanghai during the 14th year of the Republic of China. Later, in response to social needs, it was changed to a three-day publication. On May 3rd of the 15th year, it was moved to Yu for publication. Up to now, for five years, the circulation has reached more than 1,300 copies. In addition to the provinces within the country, many overseas fellow townsmen have also subscribed. Now, due to the inconvenience of printing, there are often concerns about not being able to publish on schedule. Therefore, it was moved to Shanghai for publication a few days ago. Once the various departments are set up, publication can continue.

Suspects apprehended in the Shan'ao robbery case. After the home of He Songzhao in Shan'ao, East Township, was robbed by bandits on the night of the 14th, unexpectedly on the same night, more than ten bandits appeared for the second time in the neighboring village of Wan'ao. They were discovered by the villagers, who beat gongs to drive them away. Seeing that they were prepared, the bandits fled towards Qingxian Ridge. The villagers also learned that Ye Liangen, a local, was suspected of being an informant in the Shan'ao robbery case. He was captured and sent to the county government on the 16th for interrogation.

Ningbo 75

Rui Hengxiang suffers fire, four deaths. Rui Hengxiang Candle Shop near Xinjiang Bridge in Ningbo City caught fire suddenly downstairs yesterday morning (18th) at about 1:00 AM. The shop owner's wife was awakened from her sleep and tried to escape with her children and apprentices. The stairs had broken, so she jumped out of the window and was seriously injured. Four people, including her children and apprentices, all perished in the fire. Various fire brigades rushed to the scene upon hearing the alarm and fought the fire. It was extinguished by 1:30 AM. The Rui Hengxiang Candle Shop and the Zhenmao Fruit Shop, three buildings in total, were completely destroyed, with losses of more than 5,000 yuan. The YMCA was also adjacent to the shop, but because the building was solid, it was not affected by the fire.

Railway Minister Sun Comes to Ningbo. Sun Ke, Central Committee member and Minister of Railways, arrived in Ningbo this morning (18th) at 6:00 AM, accompanied by Director Liu Weizhi, aboard the Xinjiangtian Wheel. After landing, Sun and Liu took a car to Fenghua Creek for sightseeing. They returned to Ningbo on the same day and took a special train to Cao'e to inspect the road administration, then went to Hangzhou.

Recovery of Weihaiwei Officially Signed 76

▲ Full text of the agreement will be published within days

▲ British Ambassador still in Beijing, will not come to Shanghai for the time being

Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting told this newspaper's reporter yesterday that after British Ambassador Lampson arrived in Beijing, he repeatedly consulted with me on the recovery of Weihaiwei. By last night (the 18th), both parties had completely agreed on all points, so the formal signing took place in Beijing that evening. As for the full text of the agreement, both parties agreed to publish it simultaneously next Monday or Tuesday. As for Sino-Russian negotiations, the Ministry only knows that Mo Dehui is scheduled to depart for Moscow on May 1st, and there is no other news. The British Ambassador is still in Beijing and will not come to Shanghai for the time being.
