A Scene of Shanghai's Sin 105

▲ Coveting to Obtain a Better Job

▲ Not Hesitating to Sacrifice a Younger Sister

▲ Chen Jinsheng Frauds and Defiles a Young Girl

▲ Such Scoundrels Should Be Severely Punished

▲ A Maiden of Graceful Bearing. Xu Jinsong, a native of Nanjing, resides at No. 19, Ruichang Lane, Tangjiawan, West Gate, while his family lives outside Fengmen, Suzhou. Xu works in a sock factory. His younger sister, Xu Guibao, is twenty-nine years old, with graceful bearing and awaiting marriage. However, she lacks means of making a living.

▲ Coming to Shanghai to Work as a Hostess. In March of this year, Guibao, being idle at home, came to Shanghai to seek a living. Going to work in a factory requires training and expenses, so her elder sister introduced her to work as a hostess at the New World Company's rooftop garden. However, as a hostess, she had to sell twenty bowls of tea each day to meet the quota. Guibao was not good at socializing and only sold seven or eight bowls a day, leading to her dismissal after six or seven days.

▲ Getting Acquainted with Chen Jinsheng. During these six or seven days, she met a man named Chen Jinsheng at the New World Company. He would visit her place for tea every day, and they gradually started talking. Chen claimed to be an old manager at the Longtou of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, with considerable influence. Guibao thought her elder brother, Xu Jinshan, was currently unemployed, and her second brother, Xu Jinsong's, business was not profitable either. She asked Chen to find them work. Chen readily agreed and inquired about Guibao's address, making an appointment for later.

▲ The Family Fawning on a Valued Guest. After Guibao was dismissed by the New World Company, Chen Jinsheng visited the Xu family in Ruichang Lane. As a result, her family regarded Chen Jinsheng as a valued guest and fawned upon him. Chen promised to recommend them for jobs. After waiting for several days without any news, Guibao's elder brother became impatient and returned to Suzhou. Guibao also planned to leave, but Chen Jinsheng suddenly arrived at this moment.

▲ Claiming Jobs Were Found. He said he had recommended Xu Jinshan for a job in the train's tea room and Xu Jinsong for oiling at the Longtou, both successfully. Xu Jinsong was overjoyed, but since his elder brother had already returned, he lamented the missed opportunity. Ma, Ding Zhengkang, Ding Wenwei, and others living with him also asked Chen Jinsheng to help them secure jobs in the tea room. Chen readily agreed to fill Xu Jinshan's position with Ma.

▲ Guibao Was Defiled. He then told everyone that each person had to pay five yuan to the accounting office, supposedly for buying hot water glasses, which would be more convenient and less prone to breakage than buying their own. Xu and the others deeply believed him, treating him like an ancestor and even urging Guibao not to be shy and to ingratiate herself with the esteemed guest. As a result, Chen Jinsheng brazenly took Guibao out on dates and repeatedly raped her in the railway hotel, without shame, but with a sense of achievement. The power of the living environment is indeed great.

▲ Introducing the General Manager at the North Station. Xu Jinsong, believing that good jobs had been secured, voluntarily quit his job at the sock factory. Guibao repeatedly asked Chen Jinsheng to expedite her brother's introduction. After several days, Chen instructed everyone to make a set of blue cloth clothes. Xu Jinsong was to wear a Zhongshan suit. After dressing up, they accompanied Xu and the others to the third floor of the North Station to meet the general manager. Xu and the others saw the sign "No Entry for Unauthorized Personnel," which increased their trust. However, after going upstairs, Chen glanced around and said that the foreign manager was not present and there was no one to translate, so they should come back another day. Xu and the others happily returned home.

▲ Over Forty Yuan Spent. Chen continued to spend time with Guibao, spending quite lavishly. About three days later, Chen told Xu and the others that each person needed to pay another five yuan as union fees. Xu and the others had no choice but to pawn their belongings and pay. In reality, he had no money for the hotel expenses, so he fabricated excuses to swindle them. In total, they were swindled out of more than forty yuan, and a younger sister was sacrificed for sexual exploitation. However, the benefits of the job had yet to be realized.

▲ Awakening from a Dream. The day before yesterday, Xu and Ma went to the station to look for Chen Jinsheng. Ma had a friend who was a railway police officer. The officer asked Ma about the situation. The officer became suspicious and accompanied them to find Chen. They then discovered that Chen was not a railway employee but an impostor. They asked him what he was doing, and Chen replied that he was just hanging around. The officer slapped him and took him to the police station. Xu Jinsong then felt like he was awakening from a dream. He had been cheated of his money, his sister had been defiled, and he had quit his job at the sock factory. He felt like he could neither live nor die. Therefore, he also went to the police station to seek justice. The police station then summoned Xu Guibao to give a statement, and they were enraged to learn about the seduction and rape. Yesterday, they were all sent to the local court for questioning. The court ordered the defendant Chen Jinsheng to be detained pending further investigation.

City Detective Team Solves the Wang Baoshan Assassination Case 106

▲ The Main Culprit Captured in Sijing

▲ Two Accomplices Still at Large

Wang Baoshan, a native of Funing who resided at No. 13, Lane 72, Xiangyanqiao Road, Outer Hongkou, and operated the Central Printing House and also engaged in the night soil business, was suddenly assassinated by an enemy on the night of February 28th of this year at 9:00 PM. The details have been reported in this newspaper. Although the Fifth District Third Sub-station arrested several suspects and accomplices at the time, the main culprit remained at large. It is now known that the main offender, Wang Ouguang, a native of Yancheng, was arrested by the City Public Security Bureau's Detective Team in Sijing the day before yesterday. The details of the arrest are described below.

▲ Investigating the Main Culprit. This case occurred on February 28th of this year. The Fifth District Third Sub-station arrested the accomplice Dai Ruzhao's wife, Dai Dengshi, his younger brother Dai Runeng, Wang Fugguang's wife, Wang Zhushi, Wang's younger brother Wang Wenxiang, and suspects Shi Fulin and his wife Wang, and witness Shi Zonglin, among others. They were sent to the Judicial Section and then to the local court for questioning. However, the statements of each person were evasive, and the identity of the main culprit remained unknown.

▲ Enmity Arising from Jealousy. The Director of the Public Security Bureau, Yuan Liang, attached great importance to this case. On the 14th of last month, he issued Instruction No. 175 (Fa Zi) to all subordinates, ordering them to strictly arrest the main culprit and bring him to justice. After receiving the order, the Detective Team's Deputy Captain Lu immediately secretly ordered the detectives in each squad to solve the case within a limited time. After detailed investigation by the detectives, it was finally revealed that the main culprit in this case was the fugitive Wang Fuguang. This was because Fuguang was also engaged in the night soil business, and enmity arose from jealousy in the business, leading to the motive for murder.

▲ Detaining the Suspects. After Deputy Captain Lu determined that Wang Fuguang was the main offender, he ordered a strict search for him. However, the suspect had already fled in fear of punishment, leaving no trace. Until 10:00 PM on the 12th of this month, Detective Chen Jiren reported that he had detained a suspect named Wang Wangao. He was immediately brought in for questioning. According to Wang's statement, he was fifteen years old and had been carrying night soil at his elder brother Wang Wankui's house. In the third month of the lunar calendar this year, around 8:00 PM in the evening, Wang Fuguang and Dai Ruzhao, whom he knew, came to his brother Wankui's house and secretly discussed the details of the assassination of Wang Baoshan.

▲ Third Master Escaped by Luck. After Fuguang and Dai met with his brother Wankui, the three of them talked secretly. He (Wang Wangao) was not suspected because he and Wankui were brothers. He then heard Fuguang say that eight people had gone to assassinate Mr. (referring to Baoshan), four were outside keeping watch, and four went inside to commit the act. After the deed was done, they went to the house of Third Master (referring to Wang Tingzhang) to assassinate him, but Third Master was out, so they did not encounter him. The rest of the conversation was spoken in a lower voice and was unclear. Finally, he heard Fuguang say that he had now moved to a new house at No. 14, Nanzhuangzi, Wusong. At that time, his brother Wankui did not reply. It was not until 1:00 AM that Fuguang and Dai left, he said.

▲ Revealing the Truth. Wangao also stated that after they left, Wankui told him not to reveal anything, or he would kill him. Until yesterday (the 12th), when he returned home from outside, Wang Tingzhang asked him about it. He told him the truth without concealing anything, he said. According to the statement, Deputy Captain Lu immediately ordered squad leader Qi Haitian to lead detectives Chen Jiren and Xu Rongfu, along with Wang Wangao, to a thatched shed in Gaolangqiao Northeast, Yangshupu, to arrest Wang Wankui. According to his statement, he was forty-two years old, a native of Yancheng. He said that the details of this case would be clear if Wang Peishan was arrested.

▲ Escaping to Sijing. Deputy Captain Lu then ordered the original detectives to take Wankui to a thatched shed near the Wuhua Silk Weaving Factory on Xiangyanqiao Road, Hongkou, to arrest Wang Peishan. According to his statement, he was fifty-nine years old, a native of Yancheng, and worked as a vegetable seller. He also said that the details of the case should be asked of Ling Sanlin. Then, they went to No. 12, Xiangyanqiao Road, Zhabei, across the street from the deceased, to arrest Ling. Ling stated that he was thirty-four years old, worked as a vegetable seller, and was also a native of Yancheng. He said that the main culprit Wang Fuguang had fled to Sijing and could be arrested there. The original detectives then went directly to Sijing and arrested Fuguang, bringing him back for strict questioning.

▲ The Origin of the Murderous Intent. The main culprit Wang Fuguang stated that he was thirty-nine years old, a native of Yancheng, and resided at No. 12, Lane 72, Xiangyanqiao Road, Zhabei, and worked as a night soil carrier. Because the deceased had always operated an old night soil business, he intended to set up a new business, which led to enmity with the deceased. He immediately discussed it with his accomplice Dai Ruzhao. Dai then came up with the idea to assassinate the deceased. On February 28th, around 9:00 PM, he invited five people, including Liu Daguansi, Zhu Zixiang, and Shi Fulin, to bring three pistols to the deceased's house. The deceased was sitting by a round table. Liu Daguansi rushed in first and fired at the deceased with a gun.

▲ A Total of Seven Shots Fired. After Liu fired the first shot, he and Dai also rushed in. Zhu and Shi were keeping watch outside. Liu fired a total of four shots, he fired one shot, and Dai fired two shots, for a total of seven shots. All of them hit the deceased's vital points. They saw the deceased fall to the ground and die. Seeing that their goal had been achieved, they immediately fled in different directions. As for the three pistols, Liu Daguansi brought them to the Hujiamuqiao and distributed them to them. After the deed was done, they returned them to Liu in a deserted area near the Nantong Yangzhou Theater on Tian Tong Road. Dai Ruzhao then opened a room on the second floor of the Dadong Hotel, and Liu went his own way.

▲ Awaiting Punishment. Fuguang also stated that after he and the others parted ways, he first fled to Qin San's house in Tanzikou to hide and find out what was happening outside. On the ninth day of the lunar month, he went to Zhang Awu's house outside the East Gate of Qingpu to help with work. Three days ago, he arrived on the boat of his cousin-in-law Chen Sankang in Sijing, where he was arrested. As for where Liu and Dai had fled to, he really did not know. After receiving the statement, Deputy Captain Lu immediately prepared a document and submitted it to the Judicial Section for review and handling.
